		// 'd' for integer
		// 'f' for float
		// optional '-' to not abs() the values
		// optional number to specify the number of decimals to print after a float
		// eg: %-2fMODIFIER_PROPERTY_BASEDAMAGEOUTGOING_PERCENTAGE% 
		// use %% to draw a percentage sign
